RESULT_SCHEMA_VERSION = "1.0"


def _parse_optional_bool(value: Any) -> bool | None:
    if value is None:
        return None
    if isinstance(value, bool):
        return value
    text = str(value).strip().lower()
    if not text:
        return None
    if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
        return True
    if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
        return False
    return None


def _should_start_embedded_worker(cfg: Any) -> bool:
    env_value = _parse_optional_bool(os.getenv("CLONECUT_API_START_WORKER"))
    if env_value is not None:
        return env_value

    raw = getattr(cfg, "raw", None)
    if isinstance(raw, dict):
        api_cfg = raw.get("api", {}) or {}
        cfg_value = _parse_optional_bool(
            api_cfg.get("start_worker", api_cfg.get("start_embedded_worker"))
        )
        if cfg_value is not None:
            return cfg_value

    return False


def create_app(service: WorkerService) -> Flask:
    app = Flask(
        __name__,
        template_folder=str(TEMPLATE_DIR),
        static_folder=str(STATIC_DIR),
        static_url_path="/web/static",
    )
    if app.jinja_loader is not None:
        app.jinja_loader = ChoiceLoader([app.jinja_loader, FileSystemLoader(str(TEMPLATE_DIR))])

    _api_token: str = os.getenv("CLONECUT_API_TOKEN", "").strip()
    _web_mock_mode = os.getenv("CLONECUT_WEB_MOCK_MODE", "").strip().lower() == "true"
    _api_upload_root = Path(getattr(service.config, "input_dir", "input")) / "_api_uploads"
    _api_upload_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    def _mock_mode_from_request() -> bool:
        if _web_mock_mode:
            return True
        raw = request.args.get("mock", "").strip().lower()
        return raw in {"1", "true", "yes"}

    def _parse_optional_bool(value: Any) -> Any:
        if value is None:
            return None
        if isinstance(value, bool):
            return value
        text = str(value).strip().lower()
        if not text:
            return None
        if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
            return True
        if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
            return False
        return None

    def _parse_json_object_field(field_name: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        raw = str(request.form.get(field_name, "") or "").strip()
        if not raw:
            return {}
        try:
            parsed = json.loads(raw)
        except Exception as exc:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid {field_name}: {exc}") from exc
        if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
            raise ValueError(f"invalid {field_name}: expected JSON object")
        return dict(parsed)

    def _resolve_download_path(task: dict[str, Any]) -> Path | None:
        result = task.get("result") if isinstance(task.get("result"), dict) else {}
        artifacts = result.get("artifacts") if isinstance(result.get("artifacts"), list) else []
        for artifact in artifacts:
            if not isinstance(artifact, dict) or not artifact.get("is_primary"):
                continue
            candidate = str(artifact.get("path") or "").strip()
            if not candidate:
                continue
            path = Path(candidate)
            if path.exists() and path.is_file():
                return path
        upload = result.get("upload") if isinstance(result.get("upload"), dict) else {}
        candidates = [
            str(upload.get("uploaded_path") or "").strip(),
            str(task.get("output_path") or "").strip(),
            str(result.get("named_output_path") or "").strip(),
            str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip(),
        ]
        for candidate in candidates:
            if not candidate:
                continue
            path = Path(candidate)
            if path.exists() and path.is_file():
                return path
        return None

    def _build_status_url(task_id: str) -> str:
        return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}"

    def _build_download_url(task_id: str) -> str:
        return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/download"

    def _build_artifacts_url(task_id: str) -> str:
        return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/artifacts"

    def _build_artifact_download_url(task_id: str, artifact_id: str) -> str:
        return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/artifacts/{artifact_id}/download"

    def _build_task_result_url(task_id: str) -> str:
        return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/result"

    def _find_task_artifact(task: dict[str, Any], artifact_id: str) -> dict[str, Any] | None:
        result = task.get("result") if isinstance(task.get("result"), dict) else {}
        artifacts = result.get("artifacts") if isinstance(result.get("artifacts"), list) else []
        target = str(artifact_id or "").strip()
        if not target:
            return None
        for artifact in artifacts:
            if not isinstance(artifact, dict):
                continue
            if str(artifact.get("artifact_id") or "").strip() == target:
                return artifact
        return None

    def _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id: dict[str, dict[str, Any]], artifact_id: str) -> dict[str, Any] | None:
        target = str(artifact_id or "").strip()
        if not target:
            return None
        artifact = artifacts_by_id.get(target)
        if not isinstance(artifact, dict):
            return None
        return {
            "artifact_id": target,
            "role": artifact.get("role"),
            "kind": artifact.get("kind"),
            "filename": artifact.get("filename"),
            "path": artifact.get("path"),
            "relative_path": artifact.get("relative_path"),
            "download_url": artifact.get("download_url"),
            "is_primary": bool(artifact.get("is_primary")),
        }

    def _build_task_result(task: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        decorated = _decorate_task_for_api(task, include_task_result=False)
        task_id = str(decorated.get("task_id") or "").strip()
        result = decorated.get("result") if isinstance(decorated.get("result"), dict) else {}
        render_manifest = result.get("render_manifest") if isinstance(result.get("render_manifest"), dict) else {}
        artifacts = result.get("artifacts") if isinstance(result.get("artifacts"), list) else []
        artifacts_by_id = {
            str(item.get("artifact_id") or "").strip(): item
            for item in artifacts
            if isinstance(item, dict) and str(item.get("artifact_id") or "").strip()
        }
        videos = render_manifest.get("videos") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("videos"), dict) else {}
        subtitles = render_manifest.get("subtitles") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("subtitles"), dict) else {}
        texts = render_manifest.get("texts") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("texts"), dict) else {}
        context = render_manifest.get("context") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("context"), dict) else {}
        cover = render_manifest.get("cover") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("cover"), dict) else {}
        logs = render_manifest.get("logs") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("logs"), dict) else {}
        pipeline_state = (
            render_manifest.get("pipeline_state") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("pipeline_state"), dict) else {}
        )

        task_result = {
            "schema_version": RESULT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
            "task_id": task_id,
            "status": decorated.get("status"),
            "is_ready": str(decorated.get("status") or "").strip().lower() == "completed",
            "executed_mode": result.get("executed_mode"),
            "status_url": decorated.get("status_url"),
            "download_url": decorated.get("download_url"),
            "artifacts_url": decorated.get("artifacts_url"),
            "progress": {
                "current_stage": decorated.get("current_stage"),
                "stage_checkpoint": decorated.get("stage_checkpoint"),
                "last_completed_step": pipeline_state.get("last_completed_step"),
                "last_completed_step_name": pipeline_state.get("last_completed_step_name"),
            },
            "outputs": {
                "final_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("primary") or "")),
                "subtitled_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("subtitled") or "")),
                "no_subtitle_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("no_subtitle") or "")),
                "coverless_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("coverless") or "")),
                "alternate_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("alternate") or "")),
                "subtitle_srt": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(subtitles.get("srt") or "")),
                "subtitle_ass": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(subtitles.get("ass") or "")),
                "script_text": _artifact_ref_by_id(
                    artifacts_by_id,
                    str(texts.get("script") or subtitles.get("script") or ""),
                ),
                "clip_text": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(texts.get("clip_text") or "")),
                "cover_image": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(cover.get("image") or "")),
                "forum_post_info": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(context.get("forum_post_info") or "")),
                "processing_log": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(logs.get("processing") or "")),
            },
            "manifest": {
                "schema_version": render_manifest.get("schema_version") or RESULT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
                "primary_artifact_id": render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id"),
                "primary_download_url": render_manifest.get("primary_download_url"),
                "primary_output_path": render_manifest.get("primary_output_path"),
                "artifact_count": render_manifest.get("artifact_count"),
            },
        }
        return task_result

    def _decorate_task_for_api(task: dict[str, Any], include_task_result: bool = False) -> dict[str, Any]:
        decorated = copy.deepcopy(task)
        task_id = str(decorated.get("task_id") or "").strip()
        if not task_id:
            return decorated

        decorated["status_url"] = _build_status_url(task_id)
        decorated["download_url"] = _build_download_url(task_id)
        decorated["artifacts_url"] = _build_artifacts_url(task_id)
        decorated["result_url"] = _build_task_result_url(task_id)

        result = decorated.get("result")
        if not isinstance(result, dict):
            if include_task_result:
                decorated["task_result"] = _build_task_result(decorated)
            return decorated

        artifacts = result.get("artifacts")
        if isinstance(artifacts, list):
            for artifact in artifacts:
                if not isinstance(artifact, dict):
                    continue
                artifact_id = str(artifact.get("artifact_id") or "").strip()
                if artifact_id:
                    artifact["download_url"] = _build_artifact_download_url(task_id, artifact_id)

        render_manifest = result.get("render_manifest")
        if isinstance(render_manifest, dict):
            primary_artifact_id = str(render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id") or "").strip()
            if primary_artifact_id:
                render_manifest["primary_download_url"] = _build_artifact_download_url(task_id, primary_artifact_id)
        if include_task_result:
            decorated["task_result"] = _build_task_result(decorated)
        return decorated

    def _save_uploaded_video(task_id: str) -> tuple[Path, str, int]:
        uploaded = request.files.get("file")
        if uploaded is None:
            raise ValueError("missing file field")
        filename = secure_filename(str(uploaded.filename or "").strip()) or "video.mp4"
        suffix = Path(filename).suffix.lower()
        content_type = str(uploaded.content_type or "").strip().lower()
        allowed_suffixes = {".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".m4v", ".webm"}
        if suffix and suffix not in allowed_suffixes and not content_type.startswith("video/"):
            raise ValueError(f"unsupported video file type: {suffix or content_type or 'unknown'}")

        task_dir = _api_upload_root / task_id
        task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        target = task_dir / filename
        uploaded.save(str(target))
        size_bytes = target.stat().st_size
        if size_bytes <= 0:
            target.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            raise ValueError("uploaded file is empty")
        return target, filename, size_bytes

    def _build_upload_task_payload(task_id: str, source_path: Path, original_filename: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        payload = _parse_json_object_field("payload")
        metadata = _parse_json_object_field("metadata")
        forum_post_info = _parse_json_object_field("forum_post_info")

        for key in ("clip_text", "stage5_model_name", "stage5_file_encoding", "post_url"):
            value = str(request.form.get(key, "") or "").strip()
            if value:
                payload[key] = value
                metadata[key] = value

        stage5_use_preprocessor = _parse_optional_bool(request.form.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"))
        if stage5_use_preprocessor is not None:
            payload["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor
            metadata["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor

class _TaskThreadLogFilter(logging.Filter):
    def __init__(self, *, task_id: str, thread_id: int) -> None:
        super().__init__()
        self.task_id = task_id
        self.thread_id = thread_id

    def filter(self, record: logging.LogRecord) -> bool:
        record.clonecut_task_id = self.task_id
        return int(getattr(record, "thread", -1)) == self.thread_id


class WorkerService:
    def __init__(self, config: Any, logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None) -> None:
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.worker.service")
        self.booted_at = time.time()
        self.redis_client = build_redis_client(
            host=str(getattr(config, "redis_host", "127.0.0.1")),
            port=int(getattr(config, "redis_port", 6379)),
            db=int(getattr(config, "redis_db", 0)),
            password=str(getattr(config, "redis_password", "")),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.registry = RedisTaskRegistry(
            redis_client=self.redis_client,
            namespace=str(getattr(config, "redis_namespace", "clonecut_worker:")),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.dedup_ttl_seconds = max(60, int(self._get_queue_cfg("dedup_ttl_seconds", 24 * 3600)))
        self.queue_adapter = RedisQueueAdapter(
            redis_client=self.redis_client,
            namespace=str(getattr(config, "redis_namespace", "clonecut_worker:")),
            dedup_ttl_seconds=self.dedup_ttl_seconds,
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.use_redis_queue = self.queue_adapter.is_persistent()
        self.task_storage = self._init_task_storage()
        self.lock = RLock()
        self.stop_event = Event()
        self.worker_threads: List[Thread] = []
        self.active_workers: Dict[str, int] = {
            "download": 0,
            "process": 0,
            "upload": 0,
        }

        self.stats: Dict[str, int] = {
            "received": 0,
            "completed": 0,
            "failed": 0,
            "running": 0,
            "retried": 0,
            "zombie_reclaimed": 0,
        }

        self.max_download_workers = max(1, int(self._get_worker_cfg("max_download_workers", 2)))
        self.max_process_workers = max(1, int(self._get_worker_cfg("max_process_workers", 2)))
        self.max_upload_workers = max(1, int(self._get_worker_cfg("max_upload_workers", 2)))
        self.download_timeout_seconds = max(
            30,
            int(self._get_worker_cfg("download_timeout_seconds", 600)),
        )
        self.download_chunk_size = max(
            1024,
            int(self._get_worker_cfg("download_chunk_size", 8192)),
        )
        self.max_retries_default = max(0, int(self._get_queue_cfg("max_retries", 3)))
        self.retry_backoff_seconds = self._parse_retry_backoff(
            self._get_queue_cfg("retry_backoff_seconds", [5, 10, 20])
        )
        self.upload_retry_backoff_seconds = self._parse_retry_backoff(
            self._get_worker_cfg("upload_retry_backoff_seconds", [1, 2, 4])
        )
        self.retry_check_interval_seconds = max(
            0.2,
            float(self._get_worker_cfg("retry_check_interval_seconds", 1.0)),
        )
        self.zombie_timeout_seconds = max(
            self.download_timeout_seconds,
            int(self._get_worker_cfg("zombie_timeout_seconds", 7200)),
        )
        self.zombie_check_interval_seconds = max(
            2.0,
            float(self._get_worker_cfg("zombie_check_interval_seconds", 300.0)),
        )
        self.zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds = self._build_zombie_timeout_by_status()
        self.retry_heap: List[Tuple[float, str]] = []
        self.retry_index: Dict[str, Tuple[float, UnifiedTask]] = {}
        self.active_task_ids: set[str] = set()

        Path(self.config.input_dir).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        Path(self.config.output_dir).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        self.upload_root = Path(self.config.output_dir) / "_uploaded"
        self.upload_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        self.upload_storage_backend = str(
            self._get_worker_cfg("upload_storage_backend", "local")
        ).strip().lower() or "local"
        if self.upload_storage_backend != "local":
            self.logger.warning(
                "unsupported upload storage backend=%s, fallback to local",
                self.upload_storage_backend,
            )
            self.upload_storage_backend = "local"
        self.storage_adapter: UploadStorageAdapter = build_default_storage_adapter(
            upload_root=str(self.upload_root),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.forum_upload_enabled = self._bool_cfg(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_FORUM_UPLOAD_ENABLED"),
            bool(self._get_worker_cfg("forum_upload_enabled", True)),
        )
        self.forum_reply_content = str(
            self._get_worker_cfg("forum_reply_content", "Video processing completed")
        ).strip() or "Video processing completed"
        self.forum_settings_path = str(
            self._get_worker_cfg("forum_settings_path", "config/forum_settings.yaml")
        ).strip() or "config/forum_settings.yaml"

        self.tts_adapter_enabled = self._bool_cfg(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_ENABLE"),
            bool(self._get_worker_cfg("tts_enable", True)),
        )
        tts_engine_mode_raw = str(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_ENGINE", self._get_worker_cfg("tts_engine", "local"))
        ).strip().lower()
        if tts_engine_mode_raw not in {"local", "http", "auto"}:
            tts_engine_mode_raw = "local"
        self.tts_engine_mode = tts_engine_mode_raw
        tts_default_voice = str(self._get_worker_cfg("tts_default_voice", ""))
        tts_api_endpoint = str(self._get_worker_cfg("tts_api_endpoint", ""))
        tts_api_timeout_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("tts_api_timeout_seconds", 15)
        tts_local_sample_rate_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("tts_local_sample_rate_hz", 24000)
        try:
            tts_api_timeout = float(tts_api_timeout_raw)
        except Exception:
            tts_api_timeout = 15.0
        try:
            tts_local_sample_rate = int(tts_local_sample_rate_raw)
        except Exception:
            tts_local_sample_rate = 24000
        tts_local_sample_rate_env = os.getenv(
            "CLONECUT_TTS_LOCAL_SAMPLE_RATE_HZ",
            str(tts_local_sample_rate),
        )
        try:
            tts_local_sample_rate_value = int(tts_local_sample_rate_env)
        except Exception:
            tts_local_sample_rate_value = tts_local_sample_rate
        self.tts_local_adapter = LocalTtsAdapter(
            enabled=self.tts_adapter_enabled,
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            default_voice=os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_DEFAULT_VOICE", tts_default_voice),
            sample_rate_hz=tts_local_sample_rate_value,
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.tts_http_adapter = HttpTtsAdapter(
            enabled=self.tts_adapter_enabled,
            default_voice=os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_DEFAULT_VOICE", tts_default_voice),
            api_endpoint=os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_API_ENDPOINT", tts_api_endpoint),
            api_timeout_seconds=float(
                os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_API_TIMEOUT_SECONDS", str(tts_api_timeout))
            ),
            logger=self.logger,
        )

        legacy_internal_pipeline_requested = self._extract_optional_bool(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_USE_INTERNAL_PIPELINE"),
            self._get_worker_cfg("use_internal_pipeline", None),
        )
        if legacy_internal_pipeline_requested is False:
            self.logger.warning(
                "deprecated worker setting ignored: use_internal_pipeline=false; video tasks always use VideoPipeline"
            )
        self.internal_pipeline_enabled = True

        # --- telemetry ---
        telemetry_interval = float(self._get_worker_cfg("resource_monitor_interval_seconds", 5.0))
        report_dir = str(self._get_worker_cfg("performance_report_dir", "logs/performance_reports"))
        self.resource_monitor = ResourceMonitor(
            interval_seconds=telemetry_interval,
            disk_path=str(self.config.output_dir),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.performance_tracker = PerformanceTracker(resource_monitor=self.resource_monitor)
        self.report_generator = ReportGenerator(report_dir=report_dir, logger=self.logger)
        self.video_pipeline_config = VideoPipelineConfig.from_env(output_dir=str(self.config.output_dir))
        warm_retry_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("video_pipeline_warm_retry_seconds", 5.0)
        try:
            warm_retry_seconds = float(warm_retry_raw)
        except Exception:
            warm_retry_seconds = 5.0
        self.video_pipeline_warm_retry_seconds = max(0.1, warm_retry_seconds)
        self.video_pipeline_max_concurrency = max(
            1,
            int(self._get_worker_cfg("video_pipeline_max_concurrency", 1)),
        )
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_lock = RLock()
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_bootstrap_lock = RLock()
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_thread: Optional[Thread] = None
        self._video_pipeline_runtime: Optional[VideoPipeline] = None
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_ready = Event()
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_warming = False
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_last_error = ""
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_resources: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_ready_at = 0.0
        self._video_pipeline_runtime_active_runs = 0
        self._video_pipeline_run_semaphore = Semaphore(self.video_pipeline_max_concurrency)

    def start(self) -> None:
        if any(thread.is_alive() for thread in self.worker_threads):
            return

        self.resource_monitor.start()
        self.stop_event.clear()
        if self._should_manage_video_pipeline_runtime():
            self._start_video_pipeline_runtime_manager()
        recovered = self._recover_stuck_tasks()
        restored_retries = self._restore_retry_schedule()
        self.worker_threads = []
        self._spawn_workers("download", self.max_download_workers, self._download_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("process", self.max_process_workers, self._process_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("upload", self.max_upload_workers, self._upload_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("retry", 1, self._retry_scheduler_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("zombie", 1, self._zombie_cleaner_loop)

        self.logger.info(
            "worker adapters: tts_enabled=%s tts_engine=%s tts_http_ready=%s video_mainline=%s internal_pipeline=%s redis_registry=%s redis_queue=%s recovered=%s restored_retries=%s",
            self.tts_adapter_enabled,
            self.tts_engine_mode,
            self.tts_http_adapter.is_ready(),
            "video_pipeline",
            self.internal_pipeline_enabled,
            self.registry.is_persistent(),
            self.use_redis_queue,
            recovered,
            restored_retries,
        )
        self.logger.info(
            "worker pools started: download=%s process=%s upload=%s retry_scheduler=%s zombie_timeout=%ss zombie_by_status=%s video_pipeline_path=%s",
            self.max_download_workers,
            self.max_process_workers,
            self.max_upload_workers,
            1,
            self.zombie_timeout_seconds,
            self.zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds,
            "direct",
        )

    def stop(self) -> None:
        self.stop_event.set()
        for thread in self.worker_threads:
            thread.join(timeout=2.0)
        runtime_thread = self._video_pipeline_runtime_thread
        if runtime_thread is not None:
            runtime_thread.join(timeout=2.0)
        self._clear_video_pipeline_runtime_state(clear_thread=True)
        self.resource_monitor.stop()
        self.logger.info("worker service stopped")

    def submit(self, raw_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str, Optional[str]]:
        try:
            task = self._build_task(raw_data)
        except ValueError as exc:
            return False, "", str(exc)

        existing_task_id = self.queue_adapter.check_duplicate(task)
        if existing_task_id:
            self.logger.info(
                "duplicate task ignored: incoming=%s existing=%s",
                task.task_id,
                existing_task_id,
            )
            return True, existing_task_id, None

        self._persist_task(task)
        self.queue_adapter.remember_dedup(task, ttl_seconds=self.dedup_ttl_seconds)
        self._enqueue_task(self._initial_queue_for_task(task), task)

        with self.lock:
            self.stats["received"] += 1

        self.logger.info(
            "task received: task_id=%s type=%s queued=%s",
            task.task_id,
            task.task_type.value,
            self._initial_queue_for_task(task),
        )
        return True, task.task_id, None

    def get_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        queue_sizes = self.queue_adapter.get_queue_sizes()
        queued_total = (
            int(queue_sizes.get("download", 0))
            + int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0))
            + int(queue_sizes.get("upload", 0))
        )
        task_status_counts = self.get_task_status_counts()

        with self.lock:
            running = sum(self.active_workers.values())
            stats = dict(self.stats)
            active_workers = dict(self.active_workers)
        active_task_count = (
            int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.PENDING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.ASSIGNED.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value, 0))
        )
        status_metrics = {
            "total": int(task_status_counts.get("total", 0)),
            "completed": int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.COMPLETED.value, 0)),
            "failed": int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.FAILED.value, 0)),
            "active": int(active_task_count),
            "zombie": int(stats["zombie_reclaimed"]),
            "retried": int(stats["retried"]),
            "received": int(stats["received"]),
        }

        return {
            "status": "online",
            "is_busy": running > 0 or queued_total > 0,
            "total_queue_size": queued_total + running,
            "queue_sizes": queue_sizes,
            "queues": {
                "download": int(queue_sizes.get("download", 0)),
                "process": int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0)),
                "upload": int(queue_sizes.get("upload", 0)),
                "pending": queued_total,
                "processing": active_workers.get("process", 0),
                "completed": stats["completed"],
                "failed": stats["failed"],
                "retried": stats["retried"],
                "received": stats["received"],
                "active": active_task_count,
                "total": int(task_status_counts.get("total", 0)),
                "zombie_reclaimed": stats["zombie_reclaimed"],
                "zombie": stats["zombie_reclaimed"],
            },
            "workers": active_workers,
            "status_metrics": status_metrics,
            "task_status_counts": task_status_counts,
            "video_pipeline_runtime": self.get_video_pipeline_runtime_status(),
            "uptime_seconds": int(max(0, time.time() - self.booted_at)),
            "timestamp": time.time(),
        }

    def get_video_pipeline_runtime_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        required = self._should_manage_video_pipeline_runtime()
        with self._video_pipeline_runtime_lock:
            ready = bool(self._video_pipeline_runtime is not None and self._video_pipeline_runtime_ready.is_set())
            ready_at = self._video_pipeline_runtime_ready_at or None
            resources = dict(self._video_pipeline_runtime_resources or {})
            last_error = str(self._video_pipeline_runtime_last_error or "")
            warming = bool(self._video_pipeline_runtime_warming)
            active_runs = int(self._video_pipeline_runtime_active_runs)
            thread_alive = bool(
                self._video_pipeline_runtime_thread is not None
                and self._video_pipeline_runtime_thread.is_alive()
            )
        return {
            "required": required,
            "ready": ready,
            "warming": warming,
            "last_error": last_error,
            "resources": resources,
            "max_concurrency": int(self.video_pipeline_max_concurrency),
            "active_runs": active_runs,
            "thread_alive": thread_alive,
            "ready_at": ready_at,
        }

    def get_readiness(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        runtime = self.get_video_pipeline_runtime_status()
        ready = True
        if runtime.get("required"):
            ready = bool(runtime.get("ready"))
        return {
            "scope": "video_pipeline",
           …15909 tokens truncated…    retry_count = 0
        current_stage_raw = data.get("current_stage", metadata.get("current_stage", 0))
        stage_checkpoint_raw = data.get("stage_checkpoint", metadata.get("stage_checkpoint"))
        try:
            current_stage = max(0, int(current_stage_raw))
        except Exception:
            current_stage = 0
        stage_checkpoint = None
        if stage_checkpoint_raw is not None:
            stage_checkpoint = str(stage_checkpoint_raw).strip() or None

        metadata.setdefault("task_type", task_type.value)
        metadata.setdefault("source", metadata.get("source", "monitor_dispatch"))

            source=metadata.get("source", "monitor_dispatch"),

            status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
            priority=priority,

            created_at=datetime.now(),
            retry_count=retry_count,
            max_retries=max_retries,
            current_stage=current_stage,
            stage_checkpoint=stage_checkpoint,
        )
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)

        return task

    def _apply_video_output_naming(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_result = dict(result or {})
        output_path = str(normalized_result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
        if not output_path:
            return normalized_result

        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=metadata.get("forum_post_info"),
            payload=task.payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
        )
        if not original_filename:
            return normalized_result
        if self._is_final_output_already_equivalent(
            output_path=output_path,
            original_filename=original_filename,
        ):
            metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
            metadata["named_output_path"] = output_path
            task.metadata = metadata
            return normalized_result

        try:
            named_output_path = self._resolve_named_output_path(
                output_path=output_path,
                original_filename=original_filename,
            )
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning(
                "output naming fallback to stage output: task=%s err=%s",
                task.task_id,
                exc,
            )
            return normalized_result

        metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
        metadata["named_output_path"] = named_output_path
        task.metadata = metadata

        if named_output_path != output_path:
            normalized_result["original_output_path"] = output_path
            normalized_result["named_output_path"] = named_output_path
            normalized_result["output_path"] = named_output_path
        return normalized_result

    def _attach_video_render_manifest(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_result = dict(result or {})
        artifacts = self._collect_video_artifacts(task=task, result=normalized_result)
        if not artifacts:
            return normalized_result

        render_manifest = self._build_video_render_manifest(
            task=task,
            result=normalized_result,
            artifacts=artifacts,
        )
        normalized_result["artifacts"] = artifacts
        normalized_result["render_manifest"] = render_manifest
        return normalized_result

    def _collect_video_artifacts(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        task_dir = Path(self.config.output_dir) / task.task_id
        output_path = str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
        named_output_path = str(result.get("named_output_path") or "").strip()
        original_output_path = str(result.get("original_output_path") or "").strip()
        preferred_primary_path = output_path or named_output_path or original_output_path
        primary_resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(preferred_primary_path)

        candidate_files: Dict[str, Path] = {}
        for raw_path in (output_path, named_output_path, original_output_path):
            resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(raw_path)
            if resolved is not None:
                candidate_files[str(resolved)] = resolved

        candidate_dirs: List[Path] = []
        for raw_dir in (
            str(task_dir),
            str(Path(output_path).parent) if output_path else "",
            str(Path(named_output_path).parent) if named_output_path else "",
            str(Path(original_output_path).parent) if original_output_path else "",
        ):
            resolved_dir = self._safe_resolve_existing_dir(raw_dir)
            if resolved_dir is None:
                continue
            if resolved_dir not in candidate_dirs:
                candidate_dirs.append(resolved_dir)

        for base_dir in candidate_dirs:
            try:
                files = sorted(
                    [path for path in base_dir.rglob("*") if path.is_file()],
                    key=lambda item: str(item).lower(),
                )
            except Exception:
                continue
            for path in files:
                if not self._should_expose_video_artifact(path):
                    continue
                resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(str(path))
                if resolved is None:
                    continue
                candidate_files[str(resolved)] = resolved

        artifacts: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
        used_ids: set[str] = set()
        task_dir_resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_dir(str(task_dir))
        sorted_files = sorted(
            candidate_files.values(),
            key=lambda item: self._video_artifact_sort_key(
                path=item,
                primary_resolved=primary_resolved,
            ),
        )
        single_artifact_roles = {
            "final_video",
            "video_subtitled",
            "video_no_subtitle",
            "coverless_video",
            "subtitle_srt",
            "subtitle_ass",
            "transcript_text",
            "clip_text",
            "forum_post_info",
            "cover_image",
            "cover_manifest",
            "processing_log",
            "pipeline_state",
            "video",
        }
        selected_files: List[Tuple[Path, str, str]] = []
        seen_roles: set[str] = set()
        for path in sorted_files:
            role, kind = self._classify_video_artifact_role(
                path=path,
                primary_resolved=primary_resolved,
            )
            if role in single_artifact_roles and role in seen_roles:
                continue
            seen_roles.add(role)
            selected_files.append((path, role, kind))

        for index, artifact_info in enumerate(selected_files, start=1):
            path, role, kind = artifact_info
            artifact_id = self._build_video_artifact_id(
                role=role,
                index=index,
                used_ids=used_ids,
            )
            relative_path = self._build_artifact_relative_path(path=path, task_dir=task_dir_resolved)
            stat = path.stat()
            artifacts.append(
                {
                    "artifact_id": artifact_id,
                    "kind": kind,
                    "role": role,
                    "filename": path.name,
                    "path": str(path),
                    "relative_path": relative_path,
                    "size_bytes": int(stat.st_size),
                    "is_primary": primary_resolved is not None and path == primary_resolved,
                }
            )
        return artifacts

    def _build_video_render_manifest(
        self,
        task: UnifiedTask,
        result: Dict[str, Any],
        artifacts: List[Dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        primary_artifact_id = ""
        videos: Dict[str, str] = {}
        subtitles: Dict[str, str] = {}
        texts: Dict[str, str] = {}
        context: Dict[str, str] = {}
        logs: Dict[str, str] = {}
        cover: Dict[str, str] = {}
        pipeline_state: Dict[str, Any] = {}

        for artifact in artifacts:
            artifact_id = str(artifact.get("artifact_id") or "").strip()
            role = str(artifact.get("role") or "").strip()
            path_text = str(artifact.get("path") or "").strip()
            if artifact.get("is_primary") and artifact_id:
                primary_artifact_id = artifact_id

            if role == "final_video" and artifact_id:
                videos["primary"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video_subtitled" and artifact_id and "subtitled" not in videos:
                videos["subtitled"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video_no_subtitle" and artifact_id:
                videos["no_subtitle"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "coverless_video" and artifact_id:
                videos["coverless"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video" and artifact_id and "alternate" not in videos:
                videos["alternate"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "subtitle_srt" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["srt"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "subtitle_ass" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["ass"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "transcript_text" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["script"] = artifact_id
                texts["script"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "clip_text" and artifact_id:
                texts["clip_text"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "forum_post_info" and artifact_id:
                context["forum_post_info"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "cover_image" and artifact_id and "image" not in cover:
                cover["image"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "cover_manifest" and artifact_id:
                cover["manifest"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "processing_log" and artifact_id and "processing" not in logs:
                logs["processing"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "pipeline_state" and artifact_id:
                pipeline_state = {
                    "artifact_id": artifact_id,
                    "path": path_text,
                }
                pipeline_state.update(self._read_pipeline_state_summary(path_text))

        manifest: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "schema_version": RESULT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
            "task_id": task.task_id,
            "artifact_count": len(artifacts),
            "primary_artifact_id": primary_artifact_id,
            "primary_output_path": str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip(),
            "videos": videos,
            "subtitles": subtitles,
            "texts": texts,
            "context": context,
            "cover": cover,
            "logs": logs,
            "pipeline_state": pipeline_state,
        }
        return manifest

    def _safe_resolve_existing_path(self, value: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return None
        candidate = Path(text)
        if not candidate.exists() or not candidate.is_file():
            return None
        try:
            return candidate.resolve()
        except Exception:
            return candidate

    def _safe_resolve_existing_dir(self, value: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return None
        candidate = Path(text)
        if not candidate.exists() or not candidate.is_dir():
            return None
        try:
            return candidate.resolve()
        except Exception:
            return candidate

    def _should_expose_video_artifact(self, path: Path) -> bool:
        suffix = path.suffix.lower()
        name = path.name.lower()
        video_exts = {".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".m4v", ".webm"}
        image_exts = {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".webp"}
        if suffix in video_exts or suffix in image_exts:
            return True
        if suffix in {".srt", ".ass"}:
            return True
        if name in {"total.srt", "total.ass", "script.txt", "state.json"}:
            return True
        if name in {"clip_text.txt", "forum_post_info.json"}:
            return True
        if suffix == ".txt" and (
            name.endswith("_transcript.txt")
            or name.endswith("_ai_script.txt")
        ):
            return True
        if suffix == ".json" and "cover_manifest" in name:
            return True
        if suffix == ".log":
            return True
        return False

    def _classify_video_artifact_role(self, path: Path, primary_resolved: Optional[Path]) -> Tuple[str, str]:
        text = path.name.lower()
        suffix = path.suffix.lower()
        if primary_resolved is not None and path == primary_resolved:
            return "final_video", "video"
        if text == "total.srt" or text.endswith("_subtitles.srt"):
            return "subtitle_srt", "subtitle"
        if text == "total.ass" or text.endswith("_subtitles.ass"):
            return "subtitle_ass", "subtitle"
        if text == "script.txt" or text.endswith("_transcript.txt") or text.endswith("_ai_script.txt"):
            return "transcript_text", "transcript"
        if text == "clip_text.txt":
            return "clip_text", "text"
        if text == "forum_post_info.json":
            return "forum_post_info", "context"
        if text == "state.json":
            return "pipeline_state", "manifest"
        if suffix == ".json" and "cover_manifest" in text:
            return "cover_manifest", "manifest"
        if suffix == ".log":
            return "processing_log", "log"
        if suffix in {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".webp"}:
            return "cover_image", "image"
        if "无封面文字可自由添加" in path.name:
            return "coverless_video", "video"
        if "无字幕版" in path.name:
            return "video_no_subtitle", "video"
        if "带字幕版" in path.name:
            return "video_subtitled", "video"
        return "video", "video"

    def _video_artifact_sort_key(self, path: Path, primary_resolved: Optional[Path]) -> Tuple[int, int, str]:
        role, _ = self._classify_video_artifact_role(path=path, primary_resolved=primary_resolved)
        order = {
            "final_video": 0,
            "video_subtitled": 1,
            "video_no_subtitle": 2,
            "coverless_video": 3,
            "subtitle_srt": 4,
            "subtitle_ass": 5,
            "transcript_text": 6,
            "clip_text": 7,
            "forum_post_info": 8,
            "cover_image": 9,
            "cover_manifest": 10,
            "processing_log": 11,
            "pipeline_state": 12,
            "video": 13,
        }
        return (order.get(role, 99), self._video_artifact_role_priority(path=path, role=role), str(path).lower())

    def _video_artifact_role_priority(self, path: Path, role: str) -> int:
        name = path.name.lower()
        if role in {"subtitle_srt", "subtitle_ass"}:
            if name in {"total.srt", "total.ass"}:
                return 0
            if "stage7_correct_subtitles" in name:
                return 1
            if "stage6_5_resub_subtitles" in name:
                return 2
            if "stage4_asr_subtitles" in name:
                return 4
            if "subtitles" in name:
                return 3
            return 9
        if role == "transcript_text":
            if name == "script.txt":
                return 0
            if "stage5_ai_script" in name:
                return 1
            if "stage4_asr_transcript" in name:
                return 2
            if "transcript" in name or "script" in name:
                return 3
            return 9
        if role == "cover_image":
            if "cover_overlay" in name:
                return 0
            return 1
        return 50

    def _build_video_artifact_id(self, role: str, index: int, used_ids: set[str]) -> str:
        base = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9]+", "_", str(role or "artifact").lower()).strip("_") or "artifact"
        candidate = base
        if candidate in used_ids:
            candidate = f"{base}_{index}"
        used_ids.add(candidate)
        return candidate

    def _build_artifact_relative_path(self, path: Path, task_dir: Optional[Path]) -> str:
        if task_dir is None:
            return path.name
        try:
            return str(path.relative_to(task_dir))
        except Exception:
            return path.name

    def _read_pipeline_state_summary(self, state_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        path = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(state_path)
        if path is None:
            return {}
        try:
            payload = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        except Exception:
            return {}
        if not isinstance(payload, dict):
            return {}
        summary: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if "last_completed_step" in payload:
            try:
                summary["last_completed_step"] = int(payload.get("last_completed_step"))
            except Exception:
                pass
        step_name = str(payload.get("last_completed_step_name") or payload.get("step_name") or "").strip()
        if step_name:
            summary["last_completed_step_name"] = step_name
        output_file = str(payload.get("output_file") or "").strip()
        if output_file:
            summary["output_file"] = output_file
        return summary

    def _is_final_output_already_equivalent(self, output_path: str, original_filename: str) -> bool:
        output_file = Path(str(output_path or "").strip())
        output_name = output_file.name
        if not output_name:
            return False
        parsed = Path(self._sanitize_filename(original_filename))
        stem = parsed.stem if parsed.suffix else parsed.name
        if not stem:
            return False
        suffix = parsed.suffix or output_file.suffix or ".mp4"
        expected = f"{stem}_final{suffix}"
        return output_name.lower() == expected.lower()

    def _resolve_named_output_path(self, output_path: str, original_filename: str) -> str:
        source = Path(str(output_path).strip())
        if not source.exists():
            return str(source)

        sanitized = self._sanitize_filename(original_filename)
        if not sanitized:
            return str(source)
        parsed = Path(sanitized)
        stem = parsed.stem if parsed.suffix else parsed.name
        if not stem:
            return str(source)
        suffix = parsed.suffix or source.suffix or ".mp4"
        candidate = source.with_name(f"{stem}{suffix}")
        if candidate.resolve() == source.resolve():
            return str(source)

        selected = candidate
        index = 1
        while selected.exists():
            selected = source.with_name(f"{stem}_{index}{suffix}")
            index += 1

        shutil.copy2(source, selected)
        return str(selected)

        guessed = self._guess_download_filename(source_url)
        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
import shutil
import subprocess
from typing import Any
from typing import Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def ffmpeg_exists() -> bool:
    return shutil.which("ffmpeg") is not None


def run_ffmpeg(args: list[str], timeout_seconds: int = 1800) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    try:
        completed = subprocess.run(args, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_seconds, check=False)
        if completed.returncode == 0:
            return True, ""
        return False, completed.stderr or completed.stdout or f"exit={completed.returncode}"
    except Exception as exc:
        return False, str(exc)


def _render_title_overlay_image(output_path: str, width: int, height: int, lines: list[str]) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    # Deterministic placeholder image artifact for compatibility-only phase.
    payload = f"overlay {width}x{height} {' | '.join(lines)}".encode("utf-8")
    Path(output_path).write_bytes(payload)
    return True, ""


def run_stage8_cover(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage8 input missing")

    info = forum_post_info or {}
    raw_cover_titles = info.get("cover_titles") if isinstance(info.get("cover_titles"), list) else []
    cover_titles: list[str] = []
    for item in raw_cover_titles:
        if isinstance(item, dict):
            text = str(item.get("text", "")).strip()
        else:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
        if text:
            cover_titles.append(text)
    if not cover_titles:
        for key in ("cover_title_up", "封面标题上", "cover_title_middle", "封面标题中", "cover_title_down", "封面标题下"):
            text = str(info.get(key, "")).strip()
            if text:
                cover_titles.append(text)

    title_txt = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_title", ".txt")
    title_txt.write_text("\n".join(cover_titles) + ("\n" if cover_titles else ""), encoding="utf-8")
    output_video = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover", ".mp4")
    overlay_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_overlay", ".png")
    subtitle_for_timing = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_correct_subtitles", ".srt")
    if not subtitle_for_timing.exists():
        subtitle_for_timing = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")

    method = "title_text_only"
    overlay_duration_seconds = 0.0
    fallback_used = False
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    overlay_rendered = False
    overlay_render_error = ""
    overlay_ok, overlay_err = _render_title_overlay_image(str(overlay_path), 1280, 720, cover_titles)
    if overlay_ok and overlay_path.exists():
        overlay_rendered = True
    elif overlay_err:
        overlay_render_error = str(overlay_err)

    if ffmpeg_exists() and overlay_rendered:
        overlay_duration_seconds = 1.7 if subtitle_for_timing.exists() else 2.0
        filter_expr = f"[0:v][1:v]overlay=0:0:enable='between(t,0,{overlay_duration_seconds:.3f})'"
        ok, err = run_ffmpeg(
            ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-i", str(overlay_path), "-filter_complex", filter_expr, str(output_video)]
        )
        if ok and output_video.exists():
            method = "video_title_overlay"
        else:
            fallback_used = True
            shutil.copyfile(source, output_video)
    else:
        fallback_used = True
        if ffmpeg_exists() and not overlay_rendered:
            method = "overlay_render_failed"
        if strict:
            method = "strict_rejected"
        else:
            shutil.copyfile(source, output_video)

    strict_rejected = strict and fallback_used
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "cover_titles": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_lines": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_up": str(info.get("cover_title_up", "")),
        "cover_title_middle": str(info.get("cover_title_middle", "")),
        "cover_title_down": str(info.get("cover_title_down", "")),
        "封面标题上": str(info.get("封面标题上", "")),
        "封面标题中": str(info.get("封面标题中", "")),
        "封面标题下": str(info.get("封面标题下", "")),
        "method": method,
        "fallback_used": fallback_used,
        "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
        "overlay_duration_seconds": overlay_duration_seconds,
        "overlay_rendered": overlay_rendered,
        "overlay_render_error": overlay_render_error,
        "overlay_path": str(overlay_path) if overlay_rendered else "",
    }
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_manifest", ".json")
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(
        success=not strict_rejected,
        output_file=str(output_video if output_video.exists() else source),
        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage8 fallback" if strict_rejected else None,
        artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path), "title_file": str(title_txt)},
    )


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage8_cover(*args, **kwargs)

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import shutil
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional
from typing import Any

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def run_stage9_organize(
    input_video: str,
    *,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    keep_intermediate_files: bool,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    original_filename: str = "",
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage9 input missing")

    info = forum_post_info or {}
    candidate_name = str(original_filename or info.get("original_filename", "")).strip()
    preferred_stem = Path(candidate_name).stem.strip() if candidate_name else ""
    final_dir_name = preferred_stem or task_id

    task_root = Path(output_dir) / final_dir_name
    task_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output = task_root / f"{final_dir_name}_final.mp4"
    legacy_output = task_root / f"{task_id}.mp4"

    if source.resolve() != final_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, final_output)
    if source.resolve() != legacy_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, legacy_output)

    archive_dir = task_root / f"{task_id}_artifacts"
    logs_dir = task_root / "logs"
    archive_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    logs_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    if keep_intermediate_files:
        if stage_dir.exists():
            archive_stages = archive_dir / "_stages"
            logs_stages = logs_dir / "_stages"
            if archive_stages.exists():
                shutil.rmtree(archive_stages)
            if logs_stages.exists():
                shutil.rmtree(logs_stages)
            shutil.copytree(stage_dir, archive_stages, dirs_exist_ok=True)
            shutil.copytree(stage_dir, logs_stages, dirs_exist_ok=True)

    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage9_organize_manifest", ".json")
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "final_output": str(final_output),
        "legacy_output": str(legacy_output),
        "keep_intermediate_files": bool(keep_intermediate_files),
        "original_filename": str(original_filename or ""),
        "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
        "archive_dir": str(archive_dir),
        "final_output_dir": str(task_root),
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(final_output), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage9_organize(*args, **kwargs)
